Overview\\nThe datasource plugin query path in Grafana follows a multi-layered architecture that handles query requests, dispatches them to appropriate plugins, and returns aggregated responses. The flow consists of HTTP request handling, query service orchestration, plugin context management, plugin dispatch, and response transformation.\\n\\n### HTTP Request Handler Layer\\n**File: `pkg/api/ds_query.go`**\\n- **QueryMetricsV2**: Main HTTP handler for POST `/api/ds/query` endpoint that receives metric query requests\\n- Validates incoming request (MetricRequest DTO) with optional time handling flag\\n- Calls query service with proper context (user, cache settings, request details)\\n- **toJsonStreamingResponse**: Transforms QueryDataResponse to HTTP response with status codes\\n- Handles error responses and downstream status attribution\\n\\n### Query Service Orchestration\\n**File: `pkg/services/query/query.go`**\\n- **ServiceImpl**: Core query orchestration service implementing the Service interface\\n  - **QueryData/QueryDataNew**: Entry points for query execution with optional per-query time range support\\n  - **parseMetricRequest**: Parses incoming requests and groups queries by datasource UID\\n    - Validates datasources exist and user has access\\n    - Handles expression datasources (e.g., \\\"__expr__\\\") vs regular datasources\\n    - Extracts time ranges, intervals, max data points, and query types\\n  - **handleQuerySingleDatasource**: Processes queries for a single datasource\\n    - Creates backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n    - Builds plugin context using pluginContextProvider\\n    - Routes to plugin client or query-service flow based on feature toggles\\n  - **handleExpressions**: Processes expression queries by building expression request objects\\n  - **executeConcurrentQueries**: Executes queries to multiple datasources in parallel\\n  - **getDataSourceFromQuery**: Resolves datasources from query, handling special types (expressions, Grafana DS)\\n\\n### Plugin Context Provider\\n**File: `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/provider.go`**\\n- **Provider**: Creates and manages backend.PluginContext for datasource plugins\\n- **GetWithDataSource**: Builds plugin context containing:\\n  - Plugin ID and version\\n  - Datasource instance settings (name, UID, type, configuration)\\n  - User identity and organization\\n  - Grafana configuration and feature flags\\n\\n### Plugin Client (Dispatcher)\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`**\\n- **Service**: Implements plugins.Client interface for plugin dispatch\\n- **QueryData**: Routes queries to registered plugins\\n  - Resolves plugin from registry using plugin ID and version\\n  - Invokes plugin's QueryData method\\n  - Handles errors (grpc status, context cancellation, plugin unavailability)\\n  - Sets RefID on returned frames if not already set\\n  - Returns QueryDataResponse with aggregated results\\n\\n### Plugin Implementation Layer\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/plugins.go`**\\n- **Plugin**: Represents a backend plugin implementation\\n  - Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n  - **QueryData**: Dispatches to actual plugin client implementation (gRPC or process-based)\\n  - Manages plugin lifecycle and client connection\\n\\n### Datasource-Specific Query Handlers\\nEach datasource plugin implements the backend.QueryDataHandler interface:\\n- **Loki** (`pkg/tsdb/loki/loki.go`): Time series and log querying with LogQL support\\n- **Tempo** (`pkg/tsdb/tempo/tempo.go`): Trace querying with trace search and span search\\n- **Jaeger** (`pkg/tsdb/jaeger/jaeger.go`): Jaeger trace backend support\\n- **Zipkin** (`pkg/tsdb/zipkin/zipkin.go`): Zipkin trace backend support\\n- **Graphite** (`pkg/tsdb/graphite/graphite.go`): Graphite metric querying\\n- **Parca** (`pkg/tsdb/parca/plugin.go`, `pkg/tsdb/parca/service.go`): Profiling data support\\n- **PostgreSQL** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-postgresql-datasource/postgres_service.go`): SQL querying via pgx/sql drivers\\n- **MySQL** (`pkg/tsdb/mysql/mysql_service.go`): SQL querying via MySQL driver\\n- **Testdata** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-testdata-datasource/testdata.go`): Testing and demo data\\n- **Grafana DS** (`pkg/tsdb/grafanads/grafana.go`): Internal datasource queries\\n\\nEach service:\\n- Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n- Receives backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n- Returns backend.QueryDataResponse with frames and error details\\n- Handles datasource-specific transformations and error handling\\n\\n### Expression Service (Query Transformation)\\n**File: `pkg/expr/service.go`** and **`pkg/expr/transform.go`**\\n- **Service**: Handles server-side expressions and transformations\\n- **TransformData**: Processes expression requests\\n  - Builds expression pipeline from request\\n  - Executes pipeline with data from datasource queries\\n  - Returns aggregated response\\n- **ExecutePipeline**: Runs expression nodes and transforms data\\n- **ResultConverter** (`pkg/expr/converter.go`): Converts datasource-specific responses to standardized format\\n\\n### Response Transformation\\n- **backend.NewQueryDataResponse()**: Creates standard response container\\n- **backend.DataResponse**: Contains frames (data.Frame), error details, and metadata\\n- Response aggregation in query service combines responses from multiple datasources\\n- Status code determination based on presence of errors in responses\\n\\n### Query Registry and API Server Integration\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`**\\n- Implements Kubernetes-style query API endpoint\\n- Integrates with datasource API servers\\n- Routes queries through new query service architecture\\n\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`**\\n- Builds datasource API endpoints\\n- Manages datasource-specific querying through API servers\\n\\n### Middleware and Instrumentation\\n- **Caching Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`): Query result caching\\n- **Tracing Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/tracing_middleware.go`): OpenTelemetry tracing\\n- **Contextual Logger Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/contextual_logger_middleware.go`): Context-aware logging\\n\\n### Request Flow Summary\\n1. HTTP request arrives at `/api/ds/query` endpoint (QueryMetricsV2)\\n2. Query service parses MetricRequest and groups queries by datasource\\n3. For single datasource: CreatePluginContext → PluginClient.QueryData → Plugin.QueryData\\n4. For multiple datasources: Execute concurrently with error recovery\\n5. For expressions: Build expression request → ExprService.TransformData → ResultConverter\\n6. Aggregate responses and return as JSON with appropriate HTTP status code\\n7. Middleware layers handle caching, tracing, and logging at plugin client level\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1633,"cache_read_input_tokens":115032,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1633},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"4a3fadec-87dd-46a7-9e6c-4b7f1a708716","uuid":"93dd5683-25f5-4c2b-a528-b0017fdd8291"}

Overview\\nThe datasource plugin query path in Grafana follows a multi-layered architecture that handles query requests, dispatches them to appropriate plugins, and returns aggregated responses. The flow consists of HTTP request handling, query service orchestration, plugin context management, plugin dispatch, and response transformation.\\n\\n### HTTP Request Handler Layer\\n**File: `pkg/api/ds_query.go`**\\n- **QueryMetricsV2**: Main HTTP handler for POST `/api/ds/query` endpoint that receives metric query requests\\n- Validates incoming request (MetricRequest DTO) with optional time handling flag\\n- Calls query service with proper context (user, cache settings, request details)\\n- **toJsonStreamingResponse**: Transforms QueryDataResponse to HTTP response with status codes\\n- Handles error responses and downstream status attribution\\n\\n### Query Service Orchestration\\n**File: `pkg/services/query/query.go`**\\n- **ServiceImpl**: Core query orchestration service implementing the Service interface\\n  - **QueryData/QueryDataNew**: Entry points for query execution with optional per-query time range support\\n  - **parseMetricRequest**: Parses incoming requests and groups queries by datasource UID\\n    - Validates datasources exist and user has access\\n    - Handles expression datasources (e.g., \\\"__expr__\\\") vs regular datasources\\n    - Extracts time ranges, intervals, max data points, and query types\\n  - **handleQuerySingleDatasource**: Processes queries for a single datasource\\n    - Creates backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n    - Builds plugin context using pluginContextProvider\\n    - Routes to plugin client or query-service flow based on feature toggles\\n  - **handleExpressions**: Processes expression queries by building expression request objects\\n  - **executeConcurrentQueries**: Executes queries to multiple datasources in parallel\\n  - **getDataSourceFromQuery**: Resolves datasources from query, handling special types (expressions, Grafana DS)\\n\\n### Plugin Context Provider\\n**File: `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/provider.go`**\\n- **Provider**: Creates and manages backend.PluginContext for datasource plugins\\n- **GetWithDataSource**: Builds plugin context containing:\\n  - Plugin ID and version\\n  - Datasource instance settings (name, UID, type, configuration)\\n  - User identity and organization\\n  - Grafana configuration and feature flags\\n\\n### Plugin Client (Dispatcher)\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`**\\n- **Service**: Implements plugins.Client interface for plugin dispatch\\n- **QueryData**: Routes queries to registered plugins\\n  - Resolves plugin from registry using plugin ID and version\\n  - Invokes plugin's QueryData method\\n  - Handles errors (grpc status, context cancellation, plugin unavailability)\\n  - Sets RefID on returned frames if not already set\\n  - Returns QueryDataResponse with aggregated results\\n\\n### Plugin Implementation Layer\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/plugins.go`**\\n- **Plugin**: Represents a backend plugin implementation\\n  - Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n  - **QueryData**: Dispatches to actual plugin client implementation (gRPC or process-based)\\n  - Manages plugin lifecycle and client connection\\n\\n### Datasource-Specific Query Handlers\\nEach datasource plugin implements the backend.QueryDataHandler interface:\\n- **Loki** (`pkg/tsdb/loki/loki.go`): Time series and log querying with LogQL support\\n- **Tempo** (`pkg/tsdb/tempo/tempo.go`): Trace querying with trace search and span search\\n- **Jaeger** (`pkg/tsdb/jaeger/jaeger.go`): Jaeger trace backend support\\n- **Zipkin** (`pkg/tsdb/zipkin/zipkin.go`): Zipkin trace backend support\\n- **Graphite** (`pkg/tsdb/graphite/graphite.go`): Graphite metric querying\\n- **Parca** (`pkg/tsdb/parca/plugin.go`, `pkg/tsdb/parca/service.go`): Profiling data support\\n- **PostgreSQL** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-postgresql-datasource/postgres_service.go`): SQL querying via pgx/sql drivers\\n- **MySQL** (`pkg/tsdb/mysql/mysql_service.go`): SQL querying via MySQL driver\\n- **Testdata** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-testdata-datasource/testdata.go`): Testing and demo data\\n- **Grafana DS** (`pkg/tsdb/grafanads/grafana.go`): Internal datasource queries\\n\\nEach service:\\n- Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n- Receives backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n- Returns backend.QueryDataResponse with frames and error details\\n- Handles datasource-specific transformations and error handling\\n\\n### Expression Service (Query Transformation)\\n**File: `pkg/expr/service.go`** and **`pkg/expr/transform.go`**\\n- **Service**: Handles server-side expressions and transformations\\n- **TransformData**: Processes expression requests\\n  - Builds expression pipeline from request\\n  - Executes pipeline with data from datasource queries\\n  - Returns aggregated response\\n- **ExecutePipeline**: Runs expression nodes and transforms data\\n- **ResultConverter** (`pkg/expr/converter.go`): Converts datasource-specific responses to standardized format\\n\\n### Response Transformation\\n- **backend.NewQueryDataResponse()**: Creates standard response container\\n- **backend.DataResponse**: Contains frames (data.Frame), error details, and metadata\\n- Response aggregation in query service combines responses from multiple datasources\\n- Status code determination based on presence of errors in responses\\n\\n### Query Registry and API Server Integration\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`**\\n- Implements Kubernetes-style query API endpoint\\n- Integrates with datasource API servers\\n- Routes queries through new query service architecture\\n\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`**\\n- Builds datasource API endpoints\\n- Manages datasource-specific querying through API servers\\n\\n### Middleware and Instrumentation\\n- **Caching Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`): Query result caching\\n- **Tracing Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/tracing_middleware.go`): OpenTelemetry tracing\\n- **Contextual Logger Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/contextual_logger_middleware.go`): Context-aware logging\\n\\n### Request Flow Summary\\n1. HTTP request arrives at `/api/ds/query` endpoint (QueryMetricsV2)\\n2. Query service parses MetricRequest and groups queries by datasource\\n3. For single datasource: CreatePluginContext → PluginClient.QueryData → Plugin.QueryData\\n4. For multiple datasources: Execute concurrently with error recovery\\n5. For expressions: Build expression request → ExprService.TransformData → ResultConverter\\n6. Aggregate responses and return as JSON with appropriate HTTP status code\\n7. Middleware layers handle caching, tracing, and logging at plugin client level\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
